mysql> select FS_ID
    -> ,NAT_ID
    -> , count(mem_id)as membersCount 
    -> ,SUM(INCOME1)
    -> ,SUM(INCOME2)
    -> ,SUM(INCOME3)
    -> ,SUM(INCOME4)
    -> ,SUM(INCOME5)
    -> ,SUM(INCOME6)
    -> ,SUM(INCOME7)
    -> ,SUM(INCOME8)
    -> 
    -> ,SUM(INCOME1)
    -> +SUM(INCOME2)
    -> +SUM(INCOME3)
    -> +SUM(INCOME4)
    -> +SUM(INCOME5)
    -> +SUM(INCOME6)
    -> +SUM(INCOME7)
    -> +SUM(INCOME8)
    ->  AS INCOMES
    ->  
    -> ,CEILING((
    -> SUM(INCOME1)
    -> +SUM(INCOME2)
    -> +SUM(INCOME3)
    -> +SUM(INCOME4)
    -> +SUM(INCOME5)
    -> +SUM(INCOME6)
    -> +SUM(INCOME7)
    -> +SUM(INCOME8)
    -> -50)/200) AS CLASS_INCOMES
    -> 
    -> ,CEILING((SUM(INCOME1)-50)/200) AS CLASS_INCOME1
    -> ,CEILING((SUM(INCOME2)-50)/200) AS CLASS_INCOME2
    -> ,CEILING((SUM(INCOME3)-50)/200) AS CLASS_INCOME3
    -> ,CEILING((SUM(INCOME4)-50)/200) AS CLASS_INCOME4
    -> ,CEILING((SUM(INCOME5)-50)/200) AS CLASS_INCOME5
    -> ,CEILING((SUM(INCOME6)-50)/200) AS CLASS_INCOME6
    -> ,CEILING((SUM(INCOME7)-50)/200) AS CLASS_INCOME7
    -> ,CEILING((SUM(INCOME8)-50)/200) AS CLASS_INCOME8
    -> 
    -> FROM INCOME GROUP BY FS_ID
    -> ORDER BY NAT_ID,CLASS_INCOMES,FS_ID;
